<clause id="_e9cb03e2-58d8-fd33-0364-59671fa1232a" obligation="normative">
<title id="_733618dc-5916-b587-0f42-e218379c92cf">Hazard Identification</title>
<p id="_ea59674e-d365-9df2-0366-eec247afa47f">The substance poses high potential risks for human health if handled inappropriately. It is toxic by inhalation, in contact with skin and if swallowed. Exposure to ZEN may cause cancer.</p>

<p id="_0d361e79-4234-19d1-2dae-003413d21baf">DISCLAIMER: The safety recommendations given in this section are based on literature reported best practice and have not been verified by the BIPM.</p>
